***выколоть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выколоть.html>вы́колоть</a> (20310)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колоть.html>коло́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kolótʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выколоть.html>вы́колоть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výkolotʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">выка́лывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to puncture, to pierce</li>
<li>to poke out, to gouge out, to remove by poking or gouging</li>
<li>to draw (a tattoo, image, etc.) by piercing or poking</li>
<li>to cut out the middle of</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">выка́лывание</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vykályvanije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вы́кол</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">výkol</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:копать.html>копа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kopátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выкопать.html>вы́копать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výkopatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выкапывать.html>выка́пывать</a></b>)

<ol><li>to dig (a hole or depression)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:копать.html>копа́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kopátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выкапывать.html>выка́пывать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vykápyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to dig up, to unearth</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dig up, to find</li></ol>

***выкрасить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выкрасить.html>вы́красить</a> (12217)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:красить.html>кра́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krásitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выкрасить.html>вы́красить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výkrasitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">выкра́шивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to paint, to dye
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выкрасить.html>вы́красить</a></b> что́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:голубой.html>голубо́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:краска.html>кра́ской</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голубой.html>голубо́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цвет.html>цвет</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výkrasitʹ</b> štó-libo golubój kráskoj (v golubój cvet)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to paint/dye something blue</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выкрасить.html>вы́красить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выбросить.html>вы́бросить</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výkrasitʹ</b> da výbrositʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"> fit for nothing; fit for the junk heap</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выкрикнуть.html>вы́крикнуть</a> (7061)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крикнуть.html>кри́кнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kríknutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выкрикнуть.html>вы́крикнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výkriknutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выкрикивать.html>выкри́кивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to scream out, to yell</li>
<li>to call out</li></ol>

***выкроить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выкроить.html>вы́кроить</a> (22726)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кроить.html>крои́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kroítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выкроить.html>вы́кроить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výkroitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">выкра́ивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cut out (patterns, shapes, etc. in tissue or skin)</li>
<li>to shape by cutting</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to allocate (a part of an area or room)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to find (a place for something)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to have difficulty finding (the time or money to meet someone)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">выкра́иваться</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vykráivatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вы́кроиться</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">výkroitʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вы́кройка</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">výkrojka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***выкручивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выкручивать.html>выкру́чивать</a> (23785)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́крутить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výkrutitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выкручивать.html>выкру́чивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vykrúčivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вы́крутить</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to twist off, to tweak off, to unscrew
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выкручивать.html>выкру́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>руки</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vykrúčivatʹ</b> ruki komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to twist someone's arm</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wring out</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выворачивать.html>вывора́чивать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vyvoráčivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***выкручиваться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выкручиваться.html>выкру́чиваться</a> (18319)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выкручивать.html>выкру́чивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vykrúčivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выкручиваться.html>выкру́чиваться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vykrúčivatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выкрутиться.html>вы́крутиться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come unscrewed</li>
<li>to extricate oneself <i>(from)</i>, to get <i>(out of)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выкручиваться.html>выкру́чиваться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:затруднительный.html>затрудни́тельного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:положение.html>положе́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vykrúčivatʹsja</b> iz zatrudnítelʹnovo položénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to extricate oneself from a difficult situation; get out of a scrape</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выкручивать.html>выкру́чивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vykrúčivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выкручивающийся.html>выкру́чивающийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vykrúčivajuščijsja</span>)
</p>

***выкупать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выкупать.html>выкупа́ть</a> (29020)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выкупить.html>вы́купить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výkupitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выкупать.html>выкупа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vykupátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выкупить.html>вы́купить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to redeem
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выкупать.html>выкупа́ть</a></b> что́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:залог.html>зало́га</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:недвижимость.html>недви́жимость</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vykupátʹ</b> štó-libo iz zalóga (nedvížimostʹ)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pay off the mortgage; (<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> ломбарде) get something out of pawn</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to ransom, to buy out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get, to understand
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>понима́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ponimátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:постигать.html>постига́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>суть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">postigátʹ sutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:догонять.html>догоня́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dogonjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:въезжать.html>въезжа́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vʺjezžátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">одупля́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">odupljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:втыкать.html>втыка́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vtykátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вку́ривать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vkúrivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всасывать.html>вса́сывать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vsásyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to understand the greatness of
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>Ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:выкупать.html>выкупа́ешь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мою́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:музыка.html>му́зыку</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ty ne <b>vykupáješʹ</b> mojú múzyku.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">You don't <b>understand</b> the greatness of my music.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vy-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:купать.html>купа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kupátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выкупать.html>вы́купать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výkupatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:купать.html>купа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bath, to bathe, to give a bath</li></ol>

***выкупить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выкупить.html>вы́купить</a> (18033)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:купить.html>купи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kupítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выкупить.html>вы́купить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výkupitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выкупать.html>выкупа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to redeem
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выкупить.html>вы́купить</a></b> что́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:залог.html>зало́га</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:недвижимость.html>недви́жимость</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výkupitʹ</b> štó-libo iz zalóga (nedvížimostʹ)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pay off the mortgage; (<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> ломбарде) get something out of pawn</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to ransom, to buy out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get, to understand
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понять.html>поня́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ponjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:постичь.html>пости́чь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>суть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">postíčʹ sutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:догнать.html>догна́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dognátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:въехать.html>въе́хать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vʺjéxatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">оду́плить</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">odúplitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воткнуть.html>воткну́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выкуривать.html>выку́ривать</a> (26029)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выкурить.html>вы́курить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výkuritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выкуривать.html>выку́ривать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vykúrivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выкурить.html>вы́курить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to smoke <i>(a cigarette etc)</i></li>
<li>to smoke out <i>(of)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выкуривать.html>выку́ривать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лисица.html>лиси́цу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нора.html>норы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vykúrivatʹ</b> lisícu iz nory</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to smoke a fox out of its hole</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vernacular</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drive out, to get rid <i>(of)</i></li>
<li>to distil</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выкурить.html>вы́курить</a> (12050)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курить.html>кури́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kurítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выкурить.html>вы́курить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výkuritʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выкуривать.html>выку́ривать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to smoke <i>(a cigarette etc)</i></li>
<li>to smoke out <i>(of)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выкурить.html>вы́курить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лисица.html>лиси́цу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нора.html>норы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výkuritʹ</b> lisícu iz nory</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to smoke a fox out of its hole</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vernacular</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drive out, to get rid <i>(of)</i></li>
<li>to distil</li></ol>

***вылавливаемый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вылавливаемый.html>выла́вливаемый</a> (18465)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вылавливаемый.html>выла́вливаемый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vylávlivajemyj</span>)
</p>

***выламывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выламывать.html>выла́мывать</a> (29030)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выломать.html>вы́ломать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výlomatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́ломить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výlomitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выламывать.html>выла́мывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vylámyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вы́ломить</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выломать.html>вы́ломать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to break down (a door, etc.)</li>
<li>to knock out (a brick, etc.)</li>
<li>to get by breaking</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dislocate</li></ol>
